### [1] [Scaling Laws for Embedding Dimension in Information Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05062)
*Julian Killingback,Mahta Rafiee,Madine Manas,Hamed Zamani*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文全面分析了嵌入维度与检索性能之间的关系，发现随着嵌入大小增加性能持续提升但回报递减，并且对于与训练任务不太一致的评估数据，大嵌入维度可能导致性能下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着密集检索执行的任务变得越来越复杂，基于向量和内积的基本数据结构及相似度度量方法的局限性变得更加明显。研究旨在理解当调整嵌入维度时密集检索性能如何变化，以构建平衡效率与效果的新一代检索模型。

Method: 通过两个模型家族以及各模型的不同尺寸进行实验，详细描绘出嵌入缩放行为。

Result: 发现缩放行为符合幂律，能够仅根据嵌入维度推导出性能缩放定律，同时考虑嵌入维度和模型大小的联合定律也得以提出。对于与训练任务一致的评估任务，随嵌入尺寸增加性能持续改善；而对于一致性较低的任务，则观察到较大嵌入维度下性能可能下降。

Conclusion: 本研究为理解嵌入及其行为提供了额外见解，并为选择模型和嵌入维度以实现最佳性能同时减少存储和计算成本提供了一个实用指南。

Abstract: Dense retrieval, which encodes queries and documents into a single dense vector, has become the dominant neural retrieval approach due to its simplicity and compatibility with fast approximate nearest neighbor algorithms. As the tasks dense retrieval performs grow in complexity, the fundamental limitations of the underlying data structure and similarity metric -- namely vectors and inner-products -- become more apparent. Prior recent work has shown theoretical limitations inherent to single vectors and inner-products that are generally tied to the embedding dimension. Given the importance of embedding dimension for retrieval capacity, understanding how dense retrieval performance changes as embedding dimension is scaled is fundamental to building next generation retrieval models that balance effectiveness and efficiency. In this work, we conduct a comprehensive analysis of the relationship between embedding dimension and retrieval performance. Our experiments include two model families and a range of model sizes from each to construct a detailed picture of embedding scaling behavior. We find that the scaling behavior fits a power law, allowing us to derive scaling laws for performance given only embedding dimension, as well as a joint law accounting for embedding dimension and model size. Our analysis shows that for evaluation tasks aligned with the training task, performance continues to improve as embedding size increases, though with diminishing returns. For evaluation data that is less aligned with the training task, we find that performance is less predictable, with performance degrading with larger embedding dimensions for certain tasks. We hope our work provides additional insight into the limitations of embeddings and their behavior as well as offers a practical guide for selecting model and embedding dimension to achieve optimal performance with reduced storage and compute costs.

</details>


### [2] [RAG without Forgetting: Continual Query-Infused Key Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05152)
*Yuntong Hu,Sha Li,Naren Ramakrishnan,Liang Zhao*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出了一种无需训练的框架Evolving Retrieval Memory (ERM)，通过正确性门控反馈更新检索索引，将瞬时查询时的增益转化为持久的检索改进。在BEIR和BRIGHT上的实验表明，该方法在保持原始检索速度的同时，在检索和生成任务上特别是在推理密集型任务中表现出一致的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的检索增强生成（RAG）系统虽然可以通过查询时间适应如查询扩展和迭代检索来提高鲁棒性，但这些方法缺乏状态保留能力，每次查询都需要重新计算调整且之后被丢弃，导致无法累积学习并且重复产生推理时间成本。而基于索引侧的方法如键扩展尽管引入了持久性，却依赖于离线预处理或与下游任务效用弱对齐的启发式更新，容易引起语义漂移和噪声积累。

Method: 研究者提出了Evolving Retrieval Memory (ERM)框架，它能够在没有额外训练的情况下，通过正确性门控反馈机制更新检索索引，从而把临时性的查询时优化转变成持久性的检索效率提升。ERM选择性地将原子扩展信号归属到受益文档键，并通过稳定、有界规范更新逐步进化键值。

Result: 理论分析显示，在标准相似度函数下查询扩展与键扩展本质上是等价的；并且证明了ERM的选择性更新能够收敛，可以将最优查询扩展的成本分摊到一个稳定的索引结构中，而且在推理过程中没有任何额外开销。跨13个领域的BEIR和BRIGHT实验结果表明，该方法在保持原有检索速度的同时，在检索及生成任务上，尤其是在需要大量推理的任务中，表现出了显著的一致性提升。

Conclusion: Evolving Retrieval Memory (ERM)提供了一种有效的解决方案，用于解决现有RAG系统中存在的问题，即如何将瞬态查询时的好处转变为持久的检索改善，同时避免了在线推理期间的额外计算成本。这为开发更高效、更强大的检索增强生成模型开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems commonly improve robustness via query-time adaptations such as query expansion and iterative retrieval. While effective, these approaches are inherently stateless: adaptations are recomputed for each query and discarded thereafter, precluding cumulative learning and repeatedly incurring inference-time cost. Index-side approaches like key expansion introduce persistence but rely on offline preprocessing or heuristic updates that are weakly aligned with downstream task utility, leading to semantic drift and noise accumulation. We propose Evolving Retrieval Memory (ERM), a training-free framework that transforms transient query-time gains into persistent retrieval improvements. ERM updates the retrieval index through correctness-gated feedback, selectively attributes atomic expansion signals to the document keys they benefit, and progressively evolves keys via stable, norm-bounded updates. We show that query and key expansion are theoretically equivalent under standard similarity functions and prove convergence of ERM's selective updates, amortizing optimal query expansion into a stable index with zero inference-time overhead. Experiments on BEIR and BRIGHT across 13 domains demonstrate consistent gains in retrieval and generation, particularly on reasoning-intensive tasks, at native retrieval speed.

</details>


### [3] [NeuCLIRTech: Chinese Monolingual and Cross-Language Information Retrieval Evaluation in a Challenging Domain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05334)
*Dawn Lawrie,James Mayfield,Eugene Yang,Andrew Yates,Sean MacAvaney,Ronak Pradeep,Scott Miller,Paul McNamee,Luca Soldaini*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文介绍了NeuCLIRTech，一个用于技术信息跨语言检索的评估集合，包含中文和机器翻译成英文的技术文档、110个查询及相关的相关性判断，并支持单语种检索和跨语言检索两种场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了准确衡量检索技术的进步，需要有能够有效区分不同系统的测试集。

Method: 构建了一个名为NeuCLIRTech的评估集合，该集合结合了2023年和2024年的TREC NeuCLIR轨道主题，包括原始中文文档及其机器翻译版本，并为每个文档提供了相关性判断。

Result: 创建了一个由110个查询组成的评估集，总共有35,962份文档的相关性判断，这为区分不同的检索方法提供了强大的统计鉴别力。此外，还提供了一个基于强神经检索系统的融合基线。

Conclusion: NeuCLIRTech为研究者们提供了一个新的平台来评估和发展跨语言信息检索技术，特别是对于那些希望使用更先进的初阶段检索器而不是传统BM25算法的研究人员来说非常有用。

Abstract: Measuring advances in retrieval requires test collections with relevance judgments that can faithfully distinguish systems. This paper presents NeuCLIRTech, an evaluation collection for cross-language retrieval over technical information. The collection consists of technical documents written natively in Chinese and those same documents machine translated into English. It includes 110 queries with relevance judgments. The collection supports two retrieval scenarios: monolingual retrieval in Chinese, and cross-language retrieval with English as the query language. NeuCLIRTech combines the TREC NeuCLIR track topics of 2023 and 2024. The 110 queries with 35,962 document judgments provide strong statistical discriminatory power when trying to distinguish retrieval approaches. A fusion baseline of strong neural retrieval systems is included so that developers of reranking algorithms are not reliant on BM25 as their first stage retriever. The dataset and artifacts are released on Huggingface Datasets

</details>


### [4] [Multi-Field Tool Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05366)
*Yichen Tang,Weihang Su,Yiqun Liu,Qingyao Ai*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多字段工具检索框架，以解决现有方法在处理大型语言模型（LLMs）与外部工具集成时遇到的工具文档不完整、用户查询和技术文档之间语义不匹配以及工具实用性多方面特性等问题。实验结果表明，该框架在五个数据集和一个混合基准测试中表现出色，具有优秀的泛化能力和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着可利用工具规模的增长，为了缓解LLMs上下文窗口限制并确保计算效率，有效的工具检索变得至关重要。然而，当前将工具检索视为传统即席检索任务的方法存在局限性，包括工具文档的不完整性和结构性不一致、用户查询和技术文档之间的显著语义及粒度不匹配，以及工具实用性的多方面性质等挑战。

Method: 为了解决上述问题，作者们提出了多字段工具检索框架。该框架旨在通过细粒度、多字段建模来对齐用户意图与工具表示，从而更好地捕捉到工具的功能性、输入约束和输出格式等多个维度的信息。

Result: 实验结果显示，所提出的多字段工具检索框架在五个不同数据集及一个混合基准上均达到了最先进的性能水平，并且展示出了更好的泛化能力与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 通过引入多字段工具检索框架，本研究成功地克服了现有工具检索方法面临的主要挑战，为提高LLMs与外部工具交互的有效性和效率提供了一个新的解决方案。

Abstract: Integrating external tools enables Large Language Models (LLMs) to interact with real-world environments and solve complex tasks. Given the growing scale of available tools, effective tool retrieval is essential to mitigate constraints of LLMs' context windows and ensure computational efficiency. Existing approaches typically treat tool retrieval as a traditional ad-hoc retrieval task, matching user queries against the entire raw tool documentation. In this paper, we identify three fundamental challenges that limit the effectiveness of this paradigm: (i) the incompleteness and structural inconsistency of tool documentation; (ii) the significant semantic and granular mismatch between user queries and technical tool documents; and, most importantly, (iii) the multi-aspect nature of tool utility, that involves distinct dimensions, such as functionality, input constraints, and output formats, varying in format and importance. To address these challenges, we introduce Multi-Field Tool Retrieval, a framework designed to align user intent with tool representations through fine-grained, multi-field modeling. Experimental results show that our framework achieves SOTA performance on five datasets and a mixed benchmark, exhibiting superior generalizability and robustness.

</details>


### [5] [Rich-Media Re-Ranker: A User Satisfaction-Driven LLM Re-ranking Framework for Rich-Media Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05408)
*Zihao Guo,Ligang Zhou,Zeyang Tang,Feicheng Li,Ying Nie,Zhiming Peng,Qingyun Sun,Jianxin Li*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种富媒体重排序框架，通过多维度和细粒度建模来改进用户搜索满意度。该框架首先使用查询规划器分析会话中的查询细化序列以捕捉真实搜索意图，并将查询分解为清晰且互补的子查询。接着整合候选结果的丰富侧面信息（包括视觉内容信号），基于设计好的重排序原则进行综合评估。此外，通过多任务强化学习增强模型的场景适应性。实验表明，该方法显著优于现有基准，并在实际工业搜索系统中提升了用户参与度和满意度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的信息搜索系统在提升用户搜索满意度方面存在两个主要问题：未能充分建模用户的多方面意图以及忽视了丰富的辅助信息如视觉感知信号。为了解决这些问题，作者提出了一个新的富媒体重排序框架。

Method: 提出的Rich-Media Re-Ranker框架采用以下步骤：1. 使用Query Planner分析查询细化序列以捕捉真实的搜索意图；2. 将查询分解成明确且互补的子查询；3. 结合候选结果的文字外其他丰富侧面信息（特别是视觉内容）；4. 根据多种因素（如内容相关性、质量、信息增益等）及视觉呈现效果对这些信号进行全面处理；5. 利用基于LLM的重排器根据上述原则和集成信号执行整体评估；6. 通过多任务强化学习进一步提高VLM评价器与LLM重排器对于不同场景的适应能力。

Result: 广泛的实验证明，所提出的方法相比最先进的基线有了显著的进步。特别地，当部署到大规模工业级搜索引擎时，观察到了在线用户参与度和满意度指标的大幅改善。

Conclusion: 这项工作展示了一个新的富媒体重排序框架如何有效地利用多维信号和细致的意图理解来提高搜索质量和用户体验，同时证明了其在实际应用中的有效性。

Abstract: Re-ranking plays a crucial role in modern information search systems by refining the ranking of initial search results to better satisfy user information needs. However, existing methods show two notable limitations in improving user search satisfaction: inadequate modeling of multifaceted user intents and neglect of rich side information such as visual perception signals. To address these challenges, we propose the Rich-Media Re-Ranker framework, which aims to enhance user search satisfaction through multi-dimensional and fine-grained modeling. Our approach begins with a Query Planner that analyzes the sequence of query refinements within a session to capture genuine search intents, decomposing the query into clear and complementary sub-queries to enable broader coverage of users' potential intents. Subsequently, moving beyond primary text content, we integrate richer side information of candidate results, including signals modeling visual content generated by the VLM-based evaluator. These comprehensive signals are then processed alongside carefully designed re-ranking principle that considers multiple facets, including content relevance and quality, information gain, information novelty, and the visual presentation of cover images. Then, the LLM-based re-ranker performs the holistic evaluation based on these principles and integrated signals. To enhance the scenario adaptability of the VLM-based evaluator and the LLM-based re-ranker, we further enhance their capabilities through multi-task reinforcement learning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines. Notably, the proposed framework has been deployed in a large-scale industrial search system, yielding substantial improvements in online user engagement rates and satisfaction metrics.

</details>


### [6] [SciDef: Automating Definition Extraction from Academic Literature with Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05413)
*Filip Kučera,Christoph Mandl,Isao Echizen,Radu Timofte,Timo Spinde*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 介绍了一种基于大语言模型的自动化定义提取流程SciDef，并通过新的数据集DefExtra & DefSim测试了16种语言模型在不同提示策略下的表现，发现多步骤和DSPy优化提示能提高提取性能。研究还指出虽然LLM能够从科学文献中提取出大量定义（测试集中86.4%），但未来的工作应关注于识别相关定义而非仅仅找到定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着出版物数量的显著增加，收集与任何关键词相关的定义变得越来越困难。因此，有必要开发一种自动化的定义提取工具来解决这个问题。

Method: 提出了名为SciDef的基于大型语言模型的定义提取流程；构建了两个新数据集DefExtra和DefSim，分别用于人类提取的定义及定义对相似性的评估；测试了16种不同的语言模型在多种提示策略下的表现；比较了几种度量方法的效果，以确定最可靠的评价方式。

Result: 实验结果表明，采用多步骤提示以及针对DSPy优化后的提示策略可以有效提升定义提取的表现；自然语言推理（NLI）为基础的方法被证明是最为可靠的评价手段；大型语言模型能够从科学文献中成功提取大部分定义（测试集中达到86.4%）。

Conclusion: 尽管大型语言模型在从科学文献中提取定义方面表现出色，但仍存在过度生成的问题。未来的研究方向应当侧重于如何让这些模型不仅能找出定义，还能更准确地辨别出真正相关的定义。

Abstract: Definitions are the foundation for any scientific work, but with a significant increase in publication numbers, gathering definitions relevant to any keyword has become challenging. We therefore introduce SciDef, an LLM-based pipeline for automated definition extraction. We test SciDef on DefExtra & DefSim, novel datasets of human-extracted definitions and definition-pairs' similarity, respectively. Evaluating 16 language models across prompting strategies, we demonstrate that multi-step and DSPy-optimized prompting improve extraction performance. To evaluate extraction, we test various metrics and show that an NLI-based method yields the most reliable results. We show that LLMs are largely able to extract definitions from scientific literature (86.4% of definitions from our test-set); yet future work should focus not just on finding definitions, but on identifying relevant ones, as models tend to over-generate them.
  Code & datasets are available at https://github.com/Media-Bias-Group/SciDef.

</details>


### [7] [Forward Index Compression for Learned Sparse Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05445)
*Sebastian Bruch,Martino Fontana,Franco Maria Nardini,Cosimo Rulli,Rossano Venturini*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文探讨了稀疏表示在文本检索中的应用，并通过引入DotVByte算法改进了StreamVByte压缩技术，实现了显著的空间节省同时保持检索效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索压缩技术以减少前向索引的存储占用，而不损害搜索质量和内积计算延迟。

Method: 采用了多种整数压缩技术进行实验评估，并基于此提出了新的DotVByte算法专门针对内积计算进行了优化。

Result: 实验结果表明，StreamVByte在内存占用、检索准确性和延迟之间提供了最佳权衡；而提出的DotVByte则进一步提高了空间效率。

Conclusion: 通过采用和改进压缩技术，特别是提出DotVByte算法，可以有效减少前向索引的存储需求，同时不影响检索系统的性能。

Abstract: Text retrieval using learned sparse representations of queries and documents has, over the years, evolved into a highly effective approach to search. It is thanks to recent advances in approximate nearest neighbor search-with the emergence of highly efficient algorithms such as the inverted index-based Seismic and the graph-based Hnsw-that retrieval with sparse representations became viable in practice. In this work, we scrutinize the efficiency of sparse retrieval algorithms and focus particularly on the size of a data structure that is common to all algorithmic flavors and that constitutes a substantial fraction of the overall index size: the forward index. In particular, we seek compression techniques to reduce the storage footprint of the forward index without compromising search quality or inner product computation latency. In our examination with various integer compression techniques, we report that StreamVByte achieves the best trade-off between memory footprint, retrieval accuracy, and latency. We then improve StreamVByte by introducing DotVByte, a new algorithm tailored to inner product computation. Experiments on MsMarco show that our improvements lead to significant space savings while maintaining retrieval efficiency.

</details>


### [8] [LMMRec: LLM-driven Motivation-aware Multimodal Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05474)
*Yicheng Di,Zhanjie Zhang,Yun Wangc,Jinren Liue,Jiaqi Yanf,Jiyu Wei,Xiangyu Chend,Yuan Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于大语言模型的动机感知多模态推荐系统（LMMRec），通过深度语义先验和动机理解来解决跨模态对齐中的噪声问题以及识别不同模态下反映相同潜在动机的特征，实验显示该方法在三个数据集上性能提升高达4.98%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前推荐系统在处理用户行为驱动因素时，通常将动机视为从交互数据中得出的隐变量，而忽视了如评论文本等异质信息的价值。为了克服这一限制，并解决多模态动机融合过程中遇到的稳定跨模态对齐难题及识别各模态间共同动机特征的问题。

Method: 提出了LMMRec框架，利用大型语言模型提取文本中的细粒度用户与项目动机；采用双编码器架构处理文本与基于交互的动机以实现跨模态对齐；并通过动机协调策略及交互-文本对应方法借助对比学习和动量更新减少噪声与语义漂移。

Result: 在三个不同数据集上的实验表明，LMMRec相比现有方法能够实现最高达4.98%的性能改进。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的LMMRec框架有效地解决了多模态动机融合中存在的关键挑战，为提高推荐系统的准确性和用户体验提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Motivation-based recommendation systems uncover user behavior drivers. Motivation modeling, crucial for decision-making and content preference, explains recommendation generation. Existing methods often treat motivation as latent variables from interaction data, neglecting heterogeneous information like review text. In multimodal motivation fusion, two challenges arise: 1) achieving stable cross-modal alignment amid noise, and 2) identifying features reflecting the same underlying motivation across modalities. To address these, we propose LLM-driven Motivation-aware Multimodal Recommendation (LMMRec), a model-agnostic framework leveraging large language models for deep semantic priors and motivation understanding. LMMRec uses chain-of-thought prompting to extract fine-grained user and item motivations from text. A dual-encoder architecture models textual and interaction-based motivations for cross-modal alignment, while Motivation Coordination Strategy and Interaction-Text Correspondence Method mitigate noise and semantic drift through contrastive learning and momentum updates. Experiments on three datasets show LMMRec achieves up to a 4.98\% performance improvement.

</details>


### [9] [GLASS: A Generative Recommender for Long-sequence Modeling via SID-Tier and Semantic Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05663)
*Shiteng Cao,Junda She,Ji Liu,Bin Zeng,Chengcheng Guo,Kuo Cai,Qiang Luo,Ruiming Tang,Han Li,Kun Gai,Zhiheng Li,Cheng Yang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为GLASS的新框架，通过SID-Tier和语义搜索将长期用户兴趣整合到生成过程中，以提高推荐系统的准确性。该框架在两个大规模真实数据集上表现出色，代码已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了克服现有生成式推荐系统在有效建模用户长期行为序列方面的挑战，并提高推荐准确性。

Method: 引入了SID-Tier模块来将用户的长期交互映射为统一的兴趣向量，并利用紧凑的语义码本处理大量项目空间的问题；提出了语义硬搜索方法，使用粗粒度的语义ID作为动态键提取相关历史行为并通过自适应门控融合模块重新校准后续细粒度令牌的轨迹；针对语义硬搜索中的数据稀疏性问题，设计了语义邻居增强和码本大小调整两种策略。

Result: 在TAOBAO-MM和KuaiRec两个大型真实世界数据集上的广泛实验表明，GLASS相比最先进基线模型在推荐质量上取得了显著提升。

Conclusion: GLASS框架成功地将用户的长期兴趣整合进生成过程，提高了推荐系统的性能，为生成式推荐研究提供了新的方向。

Abstract: Leveraging long-term user behavioral patterns is a key trajectory for enhancing the accuracy of modern recommender systems. While generative recommender systems have emerged as a transformative paradigm, they face hurdles in effectively modeling extensive historical sequences. To address this challenge, we propose GLASS, a novel framework that integrates long-term user interests into the generative process via SID-Tier and Semantic Search. We first introduce SID-Tier, a module that maps long-term interactions into a unified interest vector to enhance the prediction of the initial SID token. Unlike traditional retrieval models that struggle with massive item spaces, SID-Tier leverages the compact nature of the semantic codebook to incorporate cross features between the user's long-term history and candidate semantic codes. Furthermore, we present semantic hard search, which utilizes generated coarse-grained semantic ID as dynamic keys to extract relevant historical behaviors, which are then fused via an adaptive gated fusion module to recalibrate the trajectory of subsequent fine-grained tokens. To address the inherent data sparsity in semantic hard search, we propose two strategies: semantic neighbor augmentation and codebook resizing. Extensive experiments on two large-scale real-world datasets, TAOBAO-MM and KuaiRec, demonstrate that GLASS outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving significant gains in recommendation quality. Our codes are made publicly available to facilitate further research in generative recommendation.

</details>


### [10] [Bagging-Based Model Merging for Robust General Text Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05787)
*Hengran Zhang,Keping Bi,Jiafeng Guo,Jiaming Zhang,Wenbo Yang,Daiting Shi,Xueqi Cheng*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文系统地研究了文本嵌入的多任务训练策略，发现简单的批次级混洗始终能产生最强的整体性能。为解决批次级混洗在领域外泛化和增量学习方面的局限性，提出了一种基于Bagging的鲁棒模型合并方法（\modelname），该方法不仅提高了鲁棒性和效率，还在增量学习设置中显著减少了训练成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用文本嵌入模型是许多NLP和信息检索应用的基础，通常通过大规模多任务语料库训练来促进广泛的泛化能力。然而，不同的多任务训练策略在实际中的比较尚不清楚，同时如何随着新领域和数据类型的不断出现而高效地调整这些模型也是一个问题。

Method: 从数据调度和模型合并两个角度出发，对文本嵌入的多任务训练进行了系统研究。比较了批量级随机、顺序训练变体、两阶段训练以及多种合并粒度的方法，并提出了基于Bagging的鲁棒模型合并(\modelname)方法，该方法通过在采样子集上训练多个嵌入模型并将它们合并成一个模型来改善鲁棒性，同时保持单模型推理效率。此外，\modelname自然支持通过使用少量历史子集与新数据训练轻量级更新模型并将其合并到现有模型中来进行高效的增量更新。

Result: 研究表明，简单批次级混洗一致地提供了最强的整体表现，表明任务冲突有限且训练数据集大体互补。\modelname在多样化的嵌入基准测试中持续优于全语料库批次级混洗的表现，特别是在领域内和领域外(OOD)性能方面，同时在增量学习场景下大幅降低了训练成本。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了简单批次级混洗在多任务文本嵌入训练中的优势，同时也指出了其在领域外泛化和增量学习方面的不足。为此提出的\modelname方法有效解决了这些问题，展示了在提升性能的同时减少训练成本的能力。

Abstract: General-purpose text embedding models underpin a wide range of NLP and information retrieval applications, and are typically trained on large-scale multi-task corpora to encourage broad generalization. However, it remains unclear how different multi-task training strategies compare in practice, and how to efficiently adapt embedding models as new domains and data types continually emerge. In this work, we present a systematic study of multi-task training for text embeddings from two perspectives: data scheduling and model merging. We compare batch-level shuffling, sequential training variants, two-stage training, and multiple merging granularities, and find that simple batch-level shuffling consistently yields the strongest overall performance, suggesting that task conflicts are limited and training datasets are largely complementary. Despite its effectiveness, batch-level shuffling exhibits two practical limitations: suboptimal out-of-domain (OOD) generalization and poor suitability for incremental learning due to expensive full retraining. To address these issues, we propose Bagging-based rObust mOdel Merging (\modelname), which trains multiple embedding models on sampled subsets and merges them into a single model, improving robustness while retaining single-model inference efficiency. Moreover, \modelname naturally supports efficient incremental updates by training lightweight update models on new data with a small historical subset and merging them into the existing model. Experiments across diverse embedding benchmarks demonstrate that \modelname consistently improves both in-domain and OOD performance over full-corpus batch-level shuffling, while substantially reducing training cost in incremental learning settings.

</details>

### [11] [Large Language Models in Software Documentation and Modeling: A Literature Review and Findings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.04938)
*Lukas Radosky,Ivan Polasek*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文综述了大型语言模型在软件工程任务（特别是文档和建模相关）中的应用，分析了来自四个主要会议的文章，涵盖了所解决的任务、使用的提示技术、度量标准、基于人的评估方法及主要数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着生成式人工智能尤其是大型语言模型的引入，其自然语言处理能力被广泛应用于多种软件工程任务中。本研究旨在探索这些模型如何具体支持软件文档和建模活动。

Method: 通过文献回顾的方法，对从四个关键领域选取的文章进行了分析，重点关注这些文章中涉及的任务类型、采用的提示技术、评价指标、人类参与的评估方式以及使用的主要数据集。

Result: 确定了几类由大型语言模型支持的软件工程任务，并总结了当前研究中常用的方法论和技术手段。此外，还指出了该领域内存在的挑战与未来的研究方向。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型为软件工程中的文档处理和建模提供了强大的工具，但其有效性和可靠性仍需进一步验证。需要更多工作来标准化评估方法并开发新的应用场景。

Abstract: Generative artificial intelligence attracts significant attention, especially with the introduction of large language models. Its capabilities are being exploited to solve various software engineering tasks. Thanks to their ability to understand natural language and generate natural language responses, large language models are great for processing various software documentation artifacts. At the same time, large language models excel at understanding structured languages, having the potential for working with software programs and models. We conduct a literature review on the usage of large language models for software engineering tasks related to documentation and modeling. We analyze articles from four major venues in the area, organize them per tasks they solve, and provide an overview of used prompt techniques, metrics, approaches to human-based evaluation, and major datasets.

### [12] [Quality Model for Machine Learning Components](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05043)
*Grace A. Lewis,Rachel Brower-Sinning,Robert Edman,Ipek Ozkaya,Sebastián Echeverría,Alex Derr,Collin Beaudoin,Katherine R. Maffey*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对机器学习组件的质量模型，该模型旨在指导需求的引出与协商，并为机器学习组件开发者和系统利益相关者提供共同词汇，以就系统衍生需求达成一致并相应地集中测试工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多机器学习原型无法达到生产阶段，且测试通常仅限于模型属性而不考虑系统层面的需求（如吞吐量、资源消耗或鲁棒性）。现有的质量模型标准ISO 25010和ISO 25059未能充分满足机器学习组件开发者的需要，因为它们将系统属性与机器学习组件属性混合在一起，这对单独评估组件不利。

Method: 通过分析现有软件及AI系统的质量模型标准存在的不足，作者们开发了一个专为机器学习组件设计的新质量模型。这一模型经过了调查验证，参与者认可其相关性和价值。

Result: 所提出的质量模型已被成功整合到一个开源工具中，用于机器学习组件的测试与评估，证明了其实用性。

Conclusion: 本文介绍的质量模型能够帮助机器学习组件开发者更好地理解系统层面的需求，并据此调整他们的测试重点，从而提高从原型到生产的转化率。

Abstract: Despite increased adoption and advances in machine learning (ML), there are studies showing that many ML prototypes do not reach the production stage and that testing is still largely limited to testing model properties, such as model performance, without considering requirements derived from the system it will be a part of, such as throughput, resource consumption, or robustness. This limited view of testing leads to failures in model integration, deployment, and operations. In traditional software development, quality models such as ISO 25010 provide a widely used structured framework to assess software quality, define quality requirements, and provide a common language for communication with stakeholders. A newer standard, ISO 25059, defines a more specific quality model for AI systems. However, a problem with this standard is that it combines system attributes with ML component attributes, which is not helpful for a model developer, as many system attributes cannot be assessed at the component level. In this paper, we present a quality model for ML components that serves as a guide for requirements elicitation and negotiation and provides a common vocabulary for ML component developers and system stakeholders to agree on and define system-derived requirements and focus their testing efforts accordingly. The quality model was validated through a survey in which the participants agreed with its relevance and value. The quality model has been successfully integrated into an open-source tool for ML component testing and evaluation demonstrating its practical application.

</details>


### [13] [TestMigrationsInPy: A Dataset of Test Migrations from Unittest to Pytest](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05122)
*Altino Alves,Andre Hora*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为TestMigrationsInPy的数据集，该数据集包含了从unittest迁移到pytest的923个真实世界迁移案例。它为未来研究提供了基准，并支持针对Python测试框架迁移的新型解决方案的开发与验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于pytest相比unittest有诸多优势，许多项目正在从unittest迁移到pytest。但这个迁移过程可能耗时且漫长，因此需要自动化的解决方案来辅助迁移过程。

Method: 创建了一个名为TestMigrationsInPy的数据集，其中包含由开发者执行的923次从unittest到pytest的真实迁移。

Result: 提出了一个公开可用的数据集TestMigrationsInPy，能够帮助未来的自动化工具和方法的研究与发展，以促进从unittest到pytest的迁移。

Conclusion: TestMigrationsInPy作为第一个专注于从unittest迁移到pytest的数据集，为相关领域的进一步研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Unittest and pytest are the most popular testing frameworks in Python. Overall, pytest provides some advantages, including simpler assertion, reuse of fixtures, and interoperability. Due to such benefits, multiple projects in the Python ecosystem have migrated from unittest to pytest. To facilitate the migration, pytest can also run unittest tests, thus, the migration can happen gradually over time. However, the migration can be time-consuming and take a long time to conclude. In this context, projects would benefit from automated solutions to support the migration process. In this paper, we propose TestMigrationsInPy, a dataset of test migrations from unittest to pytest. TestMigrationsInPy contains 923 real-world migrations performed by developers. Future research proposing novel solutions to migrate frameworks in Python can rely on TestMigrationsInPy as a ground truth. Moreover, as TestMigrationsInPy includes information about the migration type (e.g., changes in assertions or fixtures), our dataset enables novel solutions to be verified effectively, for instance, from simpler assertion migrations to more complex fixture migrations. TestMigrationsInPy is publicly available at: https://github.com/altinoalvesjunior/TestMigrationsInPy.

</details>


### [14] [Exceptional Behaviors: How Frequently Are They Tested?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05123)
*Andre Hora,Gordon Fraser*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过实证研究探讨了在真实系统中异常行为被测试的频率，包括那些传播到测试中的异常以及未到达测试的异常。通过对25个Python系统的测试套件进行分析，发现大约21.4%的方法在运行时确实抛出了异常，并且这些方法中有接近20%是相对频繁地抛出异常。基于此，文章建议开发新的工具来支持异常行为的测试和重构昂贵的try/except块。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然当前的研究分析了传播到测试中的异常，但尚未探索那些不达测试的其他异常。为了更好地理解实际系统中异常行为的测试情况，有必要对正常和异常行为都进行测试以捕捉更多错误并避免回归问题。

Method: 研究者们执行了一个经过特殊处理的测试套件版本，监控其执行过程，并收集有关运行时抛出异常的信息。他们分析了25个Python系统共计5,372个已执行方法、1790万次调用及140万次抛出异常的数据。

Result: 研究发现，在运行时有21.4%的方法会抛出异常；在抛出异常的方法中，平均每10次调用就有一次是在执行异常行为。接近80%的方法很少抛出异常，而约20%则较为频繁地触发异常。

Conclusion: 异常行为并不总是“非正常”或罕见的情况。对于研究人员和实践者而言，需要开发新工具来促进异常行为的测试，并考虑重构成本较高的try/except结构。

Abstract: Exceptions allow developers to handle error cases expected to occur infrequently. Ideally, good test suites should test both normal and exceptional behaviors to catch more bugs and avoid regressions. While current research analyzes exceptions that propagate to tests, it does not explore other exceptions that do not reach the tests. In this paper, we provide an empirical study to explore how frequently exceptional behaviors are tested in real-world systems. We consider both exceptions that propagate to tests and the ones that do not reach the tests. For this purpose, we run an instrumented version of test suites, monitor their execution, and collect information about the exceptions raised at runtime. We analyze the test suites of 25 Python systems, covering 5,372 executed methods, 17.9M calls, and 1.4M raised exceptions. We find that 21.4% of the executed methods do raise exceptions at runtime. In methods that raise exceptions, on the median, 1 in 10 calls exercise exceptional behaviors. Close to 80% of the methods that raise exceptions do so infrequently, but about 20% raise exceptions more frequently. Finally, we provide implications for researchers and practitioners. We suggest developing novel tools to support exercising exceptional behaviors and refactoring expensive try/except blocks. We also call attention to the fact that exception-raising behaviors are not necessarily "abnormal" or rare.

</details>


### [15] [Emergence-as-Code for Self-Governing Reliable Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05458)
*Anatoly A. Krasnovsky*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为EmaC（Emergence-as-Code）的方法，旨在通过意图加证据的方式使旅程可靠性变得可计算和可控。EmaC规范声明了旅程意图，并将其与原子SLO和服务遥测绑定。运行时推理组件使用操作工件来合成具有来源和置信度的候选旅程模型。基于最后接受的模型，EmaC编译器/控制器推导出在明确相关性假设下的边界旅程SLOs和预算，并生成控制平面工件，如烧录率警报、部署门控和行动保护，这些都可以在一个Git工作流程中进行审查。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 用户体验由一系列旅程定义，其可靠性是微服务拓扑结构、路由、冗余、超时/回退、共享故障域以及尾部放大等属性的涌现特性。因此，旅程目标往往在代码外维护，并随着系统演变而漂移，导致团队要么无法满足用户期望，要么过度配置并使用临时启发式方法限制发布。

Method: 提出了EmaC的概念，它允许通过意图加上证据的方式对旅程可靠性进行计算和管理。EmaC规范指定了旅程意图（目标、控制流运算符、允许的操作），并与单个SLO及遥测数据绑定。一个运行时推理组件利用操作制品（例如跟踪和流量配置）来综合出具有源信息和置信度的候选旅程模型。

Result: 从最后一次被接受的模型开始，EmaC编译器/控制器根据明确的相关性假设（乐观独立与悲观共享命运）推导出有界的旅程SLOs和预算，并产生可以作为Git工作流一部分进行审核的控制平面产物（例如燃烧率警告、推出闸门、动作守卫）。此外，还提供了一个匿名化的构件库，包含示例规格说明和生成的输出。

Conclusion: EmaC为管理和确保复杂微服务架构中的用户体验提供了新的途径，通过将旅程可靠性与具体的服务水平目标（SLOs）和实际监测数据相结合，帮助企业更好地理解和优化用户旅程的性能。

Abstract: SLO-as-code has made per-service} reliability declarative, but user experience is defined by journeys whose reliability is an emergent property of microservice topology, routing, redundancy, timeouts/fallbacks, shared failure domains, and tail amplification. As a result, journey objectives (e.g., "checkout p99 < 400 ms") are often maintained outside code and drift as the system evolves, forcing teams to either miss user expectations or over-provision and gate releases with ad-hoc heuristics. We propose Emergence-as-Code (EmaC), a vision for making journey reliability computable and governable via intent plus evidence. An EmaC spec declares journey intent (objective, control-flow operators, allowed actions) and binds it to atomic SLOs and telemetry. A runtime inference component consumes operational artifacts (e.g., tracing and traffic configuration) to synthesize a candidate journey model with provenance and confidence. From the last accepted model, the EmaC compiler/controller derives bounded journey SLOs and budgets under explicit correlation assumptions (optimistic independence vs. pessimistic shared fate), and emits control-plane artifacts (burn-rate alerts, rollout gates, action guards) that are reviewable in a Git workflow. An anonymized artifact repository provides a runnable example specification and generated outputs.

</details>


### [16] [The Necessity of a Holistic Safety Evaluation Framework for AI-Based Automation Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05157)
*Alireza Abbaspour,Shabin Mahadevan,Kilian Zwirglmaier,Jeff Stafford*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在自动驾驶功能中，质量管理系统（QM）组件在安全相关性分析中的重要性。通过案例研究展示了即使被归类为QM的AI驱动感知系统也可能出现缺陷，导致违反风险接受标准的安全隐患。文章提倡采用全面的功能安全、预期功能安全及AI标准驱动的方法论来识别和缓解AI组件中的风险，并强调需要修订现有的安全框架以应对AI带来的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的SOTIF与FuSa分析忽略了QM组件对安全影响的严格评估。随着AI集成的发展，这些通常不被视为安全相关的组件可能带来SOTIF相关的危险风险。为了符合新兴的AI安全标准如ISO/PAS 8800，有必要重新评估这些组件的安全考虑。

Method: 通过理论分析结合实际案例研究，证明了即使是被分类为QM级别的AI驱动感知系统也可能产生可能导致严重安全隐患的非预期行为。

Result: 研究表明，必须对AI组件进行全面的安全分析和风险评估，特别是那些用于关键安全驾驶系统的感知算法中的组件。这表明现有安全框架需要更新，以便更有效地处理由AI引入的新挑战。

Conclusion: 该文强调了针对AI组件采取综合性的FuSa, SOTIF以及AI标准导向方法的重要性，以识别并减轻潜在风险，同时呼吁修订现行安全架构以确保涵盖所有组件分类下的全面安全保障。

Abstract: The intersection of Safety of Intended Functionality (SOTIF) and Functional Safety (FuSa) analysis of driving automation features has traditionally excluded Quality Management (QM) components from rigorous safety impact evaluations. While QM components are not typically classified as safety-relevant, recent developments in artificial intelligence (AI) integration reveal that such components can contribute to SOTIF-related hazardous risks. Compliance with emerging AI safety standards, such as ISO/PAS 8800, necessitates re-evaluating safety considerations for these components. This paper examines the necessity of conducting holistic safety analysis and risk assessment on AI components, emphasizing their potential to introduce hazards with the capacity to violate risk acceptance criteria when deployed in safety-critical driving systems, particularly in perception algorithms. Using case studies, we demonstrate how deficiencies in AI-driven perception systems can emerge even in QM-classified components, leading to unintended functional behaviors with critical safety implications. By bridging theoretical analysis with practical examples, this paper argues for the adoption of comprehensive FuSa, SOTIF, and AI standards-driven methodologies to identify and mitigate risks in AI components. The findings demonstrate the importance of revising existing safety frameworks to address the evolving challenges posed by AI, ensuring comprehensive safety assurance across all component classifications spanning multiple safety standards.

</details>


### [17] [Sovereign-by-Design A Reference Architecture for AI and Blockchain Enabled Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05486)
*Matteo Esposito,Lodovica Marchesi,Roberto Tonelli,Valentina Lenarduzzi*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种主权参考架构，将自我主权身份、基于区块链的信任和可审计性、主权数据治理以及在明确架构控制下部署的生成式AI集成在一起。通过将主权视为一种架构质量属性，这项工作连接了监管意图和具体系统设计，为构建可审计、可进化且具有司法管辖区意识的AI赋能系统提供了连贯的基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字主权已成为现代软件密集型系统的核心关注点，受到非主权云基础设施的主导地位、生成式AI的快速采用以及日益严格的监管要求的影响。现有的倡议单独处理治理、合规性和安全性问题，但在如何在架构层面实现主权方面提供的指导有限。

Method: 作者提出了一个主权参考架构，该架构集成了自我主权身份、基于区块链的信任与可审计性、主权数据治理，以及在明确架构控制下部署的生成式AI。此外，文章还讨论了生成式AI作为治理风险来源及其在适当约束下作为合规性、责任性和持续保证促进者的双重角色。

Result: 通过将主权视为一种首要的架构特性而非纯粹的监管目标，该研究为软件架构、生成式AI和数字主权交叉领域的未来研究与实践提供了一个有原则的起点。

Conclusion: 本文介绍的方法论不仅为理解和实现数字主权提供了新的视角，而且也为构建可审计、可进化并能适应特定司法管辖区需求的人工智能支持系统奠定了基础。

Abstract: Digital sovereignty has emerged as a central concern for modern software-intensive systems, driven by the dominance of non-sovereign cloud infrastructures, the rapid adoption of Generative AI, and increasingly stringent regulatory requirements. While existing initiatives address governance, compliance, and security in isolation, they provide limited guidance on how sovereignty can be operationalized at the architectural level. In this paper, we argue that sovereignty must be treated as a first-class architectural property rather than a purely regulatory objective. We introduce a Sovereign Reference Architecture that integrates self-sovereign identity, blockchain-based trust and auditability, sovereign data governance, and Generative AI deployed under explicit architectural control. The architecture explicitly captures the dual role of Generative AI as both a source of governance risk and an enabler of compliance, accountability, and continuous assurance when properly constrained. By framing sovereignty as an architectural quality attribute, our work bridges regulatory intent and concrete system design, offering a coherent foundation for building auditable, evolvable, and jurisdiction-aware AI-enabled systems. The proposed reference architecture provides a principled starting point for future research and practice at the intersection of software architecture, Generative AI, and digital sovereignty.

### [18] [PatchGuru: Patch Oracle Inference from Natural Language Artifacts with Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05270)
*Thanh Le-Cong,Bach Le,Toby Murray,Michael Pradel,Cristian Cadar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: PatchGuru是一个自动化技术，它从实际的拉取请求中推断出可执行的补丁规范。利用大型语言模型从自然语言描述中提取开发者的意图，并生成运行时断言作为比较程序中的补丁预言。该工具通过迭代地细化预言、识别违规行为、过滤不一致并生成错误报告来工作。在400个来自广泛使用的开源Python项目的近期拉取请求上的评估显示，PatchGuru能够以0.62的准确率报告39个警告，确认了24个真正的问题，其中包括12个先前未知的bug。与现有技术Testora相比，PatchGuru能检测到更多的bug（24对7），同时提高了准确度（从0.32到0.62）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件系统在演进过程中，补丁可能会无意间改变程序的行为。由于回归测试不完全以及补钉意图的描述是非正式且不可执行的自然语言形式，针对其预期语义验证补丁变得非常困难。因此需要一种能够从自然语言描述中自动推断出可执行补丁规格的技术。

Method: PatchGuru使用大型语言模型(LLMs)从来自真实世界的拉取请求(PR)中提取开发者意图，并合成补丁预言：这些预言是通过比较程序表达的运行时断言，它们将预打补丁和后打补丁版本集成在一起。PatchGuru通过对比打补丁前后的行为来迭代地精炼预言，识别违反行为，通过自我审查过滤不一致，并生成错误报告。

Result: PatchGuru在四个广泛使用的开源Python项目中的400个最近的PR上进行了评估。它报告了39个警告，准确率为0.62，产生了24个确认的真实正面案例，包括12个之前未知的bug，其中11个后来被开发者修复。与最先进的技术Testora相比，PatchGuru多检测到了17个bug（总共24个对比7个），同时提高了精确度（从0.32提高至0.62）。

Conclusion: PatchGuru通过对补丁意图提供可执行文档和自动化验证，补充了代码审查和回归测试。平均每个PR的成本为8.9分钟及0.07美元。研究结果表明，PatchGuru能够有效地帮助发现潜在问题，并提高软件维护过程中的效率。

Abstract: As software systems evolve, patches may unintentionally alter program behavior. Validating patches against their intended semantics is difficult due to incomplete regression tests and informal, non-executable natural language (NL) descriptions of patch intent. We present PatchGuru, the first automated technique that infers executable patch specifications from real-world pull requests (PRs). Given a PR, PatchGuru uses large language models (LLMs) to extract developer intent from NL artifacts and synthesizes patch oracles: under-approximate yet practical specifications expressed as runtime assertions in comparison programs that integrate pre- and post-patch versions. Patch oracles focus on patch-relevant behaviors, enable automated validation, and support cross-version properties. PatchGuru iteratively refines inferred oracles by comparing pre- and post-patch behaviors, identifies violations, filters inconsistencies via self-review, and generates bug reports. We evaluate PatchGuru on 400 recent PRs from four widely used open-source Python projects. PatchGuru reports 39 warnings with a precision of 0.62, yielding 24 confirmed true positives, including 12 previously unknown bugs, 11 of which were subsequently fixed by developers. Compared to the state-of-the-art technique Testora, PatchGuru detects 17 more bugs (24 vs. 7) while improving precision from 0.32 to 0.62. PatchGuru incurs an average cost of 8.9 minutes and USD 0.07 per PR. These results suggest that PatchGuru complements code review and regression testing by providing executable documentation and automated validation of patch intent.

</details>


### [19] [Does Programming Language Matter? An Empirical Study of Fuzzing Bug Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05312)
*Tatsuya Shirai,Olivier Nourry,Yutaro Kashiwa,Kenji Fujiwara,Hajimu Iida*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究分析了559个OSS-Fuzz项目的61,444个模糊测试错误和999,248次构建，发现不同编程语言的模糊测试错误特性和检测效率存在差异。C++和Rust的模糊测试错误检测频率较高；Rust和Python虽然漏洞比率低，但更倾向于暴露严重漏洞；崩溃类型在不同语言中有所不同，Go中的不可重现错误较为常见，而Rust中则较少；Python尽管有较高的补丁覆盖率，但检测时间较长。这些结果表明，语言设计对模糊测试的行为和效果有很大影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管持续模糊测试已被广泛采用，但之前的研究没有探讨过它在不同编程语言间的有效性是否存在差异。为了填补这一空白，本研究旨在通过大规模跨语言分析来考察不同语言间模糊测试错误特性和检测效率的差异。

Method: 该研究选取了来自559个OSS-Fuzz项目的大量数据集，包括61,444个模糊测试错误记录及999,248次构建记录，并根据主要使用的编程语言进行了分类。基于此数据集，研究人员分析了不同语言下的模糊测试行为模式及其有效性。

Result: (i) C++与Rust显示出更高的模糊测试错误检测频率。(ii) 尽管Rust和Python的漏洞比例较低，但它们更容易揭露严重漏洞。(iii) 不同语言间崩溃类型的分布情况各异，Go中出现更多无法复现的问题，而在Rust中这类问题很少见。(iv) Python虽然达到了较高的修复覆盖率，但在发现问题所需的时间上较长。

Conclusion: 这项研究表明，编程语言的设计对模糊测试的效果有着显著的影响。理解这种影响有助于制定更加针对特定语言的模糊测试策略以及开发相应的工具。

Abstract: Fuzzing has become a popular technique for automatically detecting vulnerabilities and bugs by generating unexpected inputs. In recent years, the fuzzing process has been integrated into continuous integration workflows (i.e., continuous fuzzing), enabling short and frequent testing cycles. Despite its widespread adoption, prior research has not examined whether the effectiveness of continuous fuzzing varies across programming languages. This study conducts a large-scale cross-language analysis to examine how fuzzing bug characteristics and detection efficiency differ among languages. We analyze 61,444 fuzzing bugs and 999,248 builds from 559 OSS-Fuzz projects categorized by primary language. Our findings reveal that (i) C++ and Rust exhibit higher fuzzing bug detection frequencies, (ii) Rust and Python show low vulnerability ratios but tend to expose more critical vulnerabilities, (iii) crash types vary across languages and unreproducible bugs are more frequent in Go but rare in Rust, and (iv) Python attains higher patch coverage but suffers from longer time-to-detection. These results demonstrate that fuzzing behavior and effectiveness are strongly shaped by language design, providing insights for language-aware fuzzing strategies and tool development.

</details>


### [20] [Can We Classify Flaky Tests Using Only Test Code? An LLM-Based Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05465)
*Alexander Berndt,Vekil Bekmyradov,Rainer Gemulla,Marcus Kessel,Thomas Bach,Sebastian Baltes*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究评估了三种大型语言模型（LLM）使用三种提示技术在两个基准数据集上的表现，以解决不稳定测试分类的泛化问题。结果表明，仅基于测试代码，LLMs难以准确分类不稳定测试，最佳组合的结果仅略优于随机猜测。手动分析也显示测试代码本身可能不包含足够的信息来进行不稳定分类。建议未来的研究应考虑提供额外上下文给LLMs来改进分类效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 之前用于分类不稳定测试的方法缺乏泛化能力，限制了其在实际环境中的应用。鉴于预训练的大型语言模型（LLM）显示出跨多种任务的泛化能力，这项研究旨在探索LLM是否能解决先前方法的泛化不足问题。

Method: 本研究选择了三种LLM（包括两种通用型和一种专门针对代码的模型），并利用三种不同的提示技术，在来自先前研究的两个基准数据集上进行评估。此外，还手动检查了50个样本，以判断仅凭测试代码是否足以让人做出正确的不稳定测试分类。

Result: 实验结果显示，即使是最优的提示-模型组合对于不稳定测试的分类也仅仅比随机猜测稍好一点。手动分析发现，仅靠测试代码往往不足以完成对测试是否为不稳定的判定。

Conclusion: 尽管大型语言模型展现出了在多个领域中的强大能力，但对于不稳定测试的自动分类来说，它们单独依赖于测试代码的表现并不理想。为了提高分类准确性，未来的研究应该着眼于如何有效地向这些模型提供更多的上下文信息。

Abstract: Flaky tests yield inconsistent results when they are repeatedly executed on the same code revision. They interfere with automated quality assurance of code changes and hinder efficient software testing. Previous work evaluated approaches to train machine learning models to classify flaky tests based on identifiers in the test code. However, the resulting classifiers have been shown to lack generalizability, hindering their applicability in practical environments. Recently, pre-trained Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown the capability to generalize across various tasks. Thus, they represent a promising approach to address the generalizability problem of previous approaches. In this study, we evaluated three LLMs (two general-purpose models, one code-specific model) using three prompting techniques on two benchmark datasets from prior studies on flaky test classification. Furthermore, we manually investigated 50 samples from the given datasets to determine whether classifying flaky tests based only on test code is feasible for humans. Our findings indicate that LLMs struggle to classify flaky tests given only the test code. The results of our best prompt-model combination were only marginally better than random guessing. In our manual analysis, we found that the test code does not necessarily contain sufficient information for a flakiness classification. Our findings motivate future work to evaluate LLMs for flakiness classification with additional context, for example, using retrieval-augmented generation or agentic AI.

### [21] [ArkTS-CodeSearch: A Open-Source ArkTS Dataset for Code Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05550)
*Yulong He,Artem Ermakov,Sergey Kovalchuk,Artem Aliev,Dmitry Shalymov*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个大规模的ArkTS数据集，用于代码检索和评估任务，并通过自然语言评论来检索对应的ArkTS函数。同时对现有的开源代码嵌入模型进行了评估和微调，以提高ArkTS代码理解能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ArkTS作为OpenHarmony生态系统中的核心编程语言，在代码智能方面的研究受到了缺乏公开数据集和评估基准的限制。

Method: 从GitHub和Gitee爬取ArkTS仓库，使用tree-sitter-arkts提取注释-函数对，并进行跨平台去重及统计分析ArkTS函数类型；对所有现有开源代码嵌入模型在单搜索任务上进行评估，并使用ArkTS和TypeScript训练数据集进行微调。

Result: 开发了首个系统性的ArkTS代码检索基准，创建了高性能的ArkTS代码理解模型。

Conclusion: 该工作为ArkTS代码检索提供了首个系统性基准，并公开发布了数据集与微调后的模型。

Abstract: ArkTS is a core programming language in the OpenHarmony ecosystem, yet research on ArkTS code intelligence is hindered by the lack of public datasets and evaluation benchmarks. This paper presents a large-scale ArkTS dataset constructed from open-source repositories, targeting code retrieval and code evaluation tasks. We design a single-search task, where natural language comments are used to retrieve corresponding ArkTS functions. ArkTS repositories are crawled from GitHub and Gitee, and comment-function pairs are extracted using tree-sitter-arkts, followed by cross-platform deduplication and statistical analysis of ArkTS function types. We further evaluate all existing open-source code embedding models on the single-search task and perform fine-tuning using both ArkTS and TypeScript training datasets, resulting in a high-performing model for ArkTS code understanding. This work establishes the first systematic benchmark for ArkTS code retrieval. Both the dataset and our fine-tuned model will be released publicly and are available at https://huggingface.co/hreyulog/embedinggemma_arkts and https://huggingface.co/datasets/hreyulog/arkts-code-docstring,establishing the first systematic benchmark for ArkTS code retrieval.

### [22] [Towards Green AI: Decoding the Energy of LLM Inference in Software Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05712)
*Lola Solovyeva,Fernando Castor*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究通过分析不同参数规模的LLM在代码生成和理解任务中的能耗模式，发现预填充成本会影响解码阶段的能耗，并且抑制冗余输出可以显著节省能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI辅助工具越来越多地融入软件开发工作流程，大型语言模型（LLMs）的使用带来了巨大的计算和能源成本。因此，了解并减少LLM推理过程中的能源足迹对于实现可持续的软件开发至关重要。

Method: 本研究对六个6B-7B参数规模和四个3B-4B参数规模的基于transformer的模型进行了分析，重点考察了它们在代码生成（HumanEval基准测试）和代码理解（LongBench基准测试）上的表现。分析分为两个阶段：预填充阶段，即模型处理输入并建立内部表示；以及解码阶段，根据存储的状态生成输出令牌。

Result: 研究结果显示，在两个参数组中，不同模型在各阶段表现出不同的能耗模式。此外，预填充成本增加会放大解码过程中每令牌的能量成本，增幅从1.3%到51.8%不等。值得注意的是，在所测试的十个模型中有三个表现出“喋喋不休”的行为，即向输出添加过多内容导致不必要的能耗增加。通过实施针对代码生成的‘喋喋不休’抑制措施，能够在不影响生成准确性的情况下实现44%至89%的能量节约。

Conclusion: 这些发现表明，预填充的成本确实影响到了主要负责能耗的解码阶段，并且通过抑制‘喋喋不休’的行为能够达到高达89%的能量节约效果。因此，为了减少推理过程中的能耗，需要同时解决‘喋喋不休’的问题以及限制预填充对解码阶段的影响。

Abstract: Context: AI-assisted tools are increasingly integrated into software development workflows, but their reliance on large language models (LLMs) introduces substantial computational and energy costs. Understanding and reducing the energy footprint of LLM inference is therefore essential for sustainable software development. Objective: In this study, we conduct a phase-level analysis of LLM inference energy consumption, distinguishing between the (1) prefill, where the model processes the input and builds internal representations, and (2) decoding, where output tokens are generated using the stored state. Method: We investigate six 6B-7B and four 3B-4B transformer-based models, evaluating them on code-centric benchmarks HumanEval for code generation and LongBench for code understanding. Results: Our findings show that, within both parameter groups, models exhibit distinct energy patterns across phases. Furthermore, we observed that increases in prefill cost amplify the energy cost per token during decoding, with amplifications ranging from 1.3% to 51.8% depending on the model. Lastly, three out of ten models demonstrate babbling behavior, adding excessive content to the output that unnecessarily inflates energy consumption. We implemented babbling suppression for code generation, achieving energy savings ranging from 44% to 89% without affecting generation accuracy. Conclusion: These findings show that prefill costs influence decoding, which dominates energy consumption, and that babbling suppression can yield up to 89% energy savings. Reducing inference energy therefore requires both mitigating babbling behavior and limiting impact of prefill on decoding.

</details>


### [23] [A Bayesian Optimization-Based AutoML Framework for Non-Intrusive Load Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05739)
*Nazanin Siavash,Armin Moin*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种结合了贝叶斯优化用于自动化模型选择及超参数调整的新型框架，并开发了名为AutoML4NILM的支持多种算法及其超参数配置的开源工具包。

Result: 成功构建了支持11种不同算法（每种都有各自的超参数）的AutoML4NILM框架，其设计灵活可扩展，既支持新增算法也允许调整现有算法的超参数。

This method provides a cost-effective alternative to installing dedicated smart meters for each appliance. In this paper, we introduce a novel framework that incorporates Automated Machine Learning (AutoML) into the NILM domain, utilizing Bayesian Optimization for automated model selection and hyperparameter tuning. This framework empowers domain practitioners to effectively apply machine learning techniques without requiring advanced expertise in data science or machine learning. To support further research and industry adoption, we present AutoML4NILM, a flexible and extensible open-source toolkit designed to streamline the deployment of AutoML solutions for energy disaggregation. Currently, this framework supports 11 algorithms, each with different hyperparameters; however, its flexible design allows for the extension of both the algorithms and their hyperparameters.

### [24] [Automated Customization of LLMs for Enterprise Code Repositories Using Semantic Scopes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05780)
*Ulrich Finkler,Irene Manotas,Wei Zhang,Geert Janssen,Octavian Popescu,Shyam Ramji*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种基于代码语义范围的自动化大语言模型定制方法，以提高模型在私有代码库上的代码补全性能。通过对比两种定制策略（检索增强生成和监督微调）在实际工业案例中的表现，证明了定制化模型能够提供更准确的代码建议，从而提高开发者的生产力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在公开基准测试中表现出色，但它们在处理未在其训练数据中出现过的私有代码库时仍然存在困难。为了改善这一情况，研究提出了一种针对特定代码库进行模型定制的方法，旨在提升代码补全任务的准确性与效率。

Method: 研究人员提出了一个基于代码语义范围自动定制大语言模型的方法，并通过检索增强生成(RAG)和监督微调(FT)两种策略对真实企业环境下的私有代码库进行了评估。该方法包括从代码库中提取信息并形成带有语义范围标签的训练数据对，以此来帮助模型学习到特定于该代码库的模式。

Result: 实验结果表明，经过适当大小定制化处理后的模型，在代码补全质量上显著优于未经定制的大规模模型。此外，还分析了这两种定制策略应用于两个公开基准的效果，并探讨了未来的研究方向。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，通过对大语言模型进行基于代码语义范围的定制，可以显著提高其在私有代码库上执行代码补全任务的表现，为开发者提供更加精确的支持，进而提升工作效率。

Abstract: Code completion (CC) is a task frequently used by developers when working in collaboration with LLM-based programming assistants. Despite the increased performance of LLMs on public benchmarks, out of the box LLMs still have a hard time generating code that aligns with a private code repository not previously seen by the model's training data. Customizing code LLMs to a private repository provides a way to improve the model performance. In this paper we present our approach for automated LLM customization based on semantic scopes in the code. We evaluate LLMs on real industry cases with two private enterprise code repositories with two customization strategies: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) and supervised Fine-Tuning (FT). Our mechanism for ingesting the repository's data and formulating the training data pairs with semantic scopes helps models to learn the underlying patterns specific to the repository, providing more precise code to developers and helping to boost their productivity. The code completions of moderately sized customized models can be significantly better than those of uncustomized models of much larger capacity. We also include an analysis of customization on two public benchmarks and present opportunities for future work.

</details>


### [25] [When Elo Lies: Hidden Biases in Codeforces-Based Evaluation of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05891)
*Shenyu Zheng,Ximing Dong,Xiaoshuang Liu,Gustavo Oliva,Chong Chun Yong,Dayi Lin,Boyuan Chen,Shaowei Wang,Ahmed E. Hassan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文系统地研究了影响Elo评分的隐藏因素，包括提交的时间顺序、比赛难度选择以及大语言模型运行间的随机变化性，并通过实验证明这些因素对评分有显著影响，强调了直接比较Elo分数的不可靠性和误导性，除非实验设置被严格标准化且透明公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型（LLMs）在复杂推理方面取得突破，基于Codeforces的Elo评级成为了评估竞技编程能力的重要指标。然而，这些评分经常在缺乏关键实验细节的情况下报告，导致了显著差异——例如最近的报道中指出同一模型版本的得分波动接近500分。

Method: 本研究采用了一套受控基准，包含了37场近期Codeforces竞赛和13,691个生成的测试案例，以此来展示Elo评分对于特定参数的高度敏感性。

Result: 研究表明，改变提交顺序可以导致分数变动达394分；而比赛选择的不同则可造成同一模型间高达1,122分的差距。此外，在评估相同竞赛时，不同次运行性能之间的最大平均分数差为349分。

Conclusion: 结论是，如果没有严格的标准化流程及实验设置的透明化报告，直接的Elo评分比较是不可靠且可能具有误导性的。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) achieve breakthroughs in complex reasoning, Codeforces-based Elo ratings have emerged as a prominent metric for evaluating competitive programming capabilities. However, these ratings are often reported without critical experimental details, leading to significant discrepancies illustrated by recent reports where the score of the same model version fluctuated by nearly 500 points. This paper presents a systematic empirical study on the hidden factors biasing Elo evaluations: (1) the temporal ordering of submissions, (2) contest difficulty selection, and (3) run to run stochastic variability of LLMs. Utilizing a controlled benchmark of 37 recent Codeforces contests and 13,691 generated test cases, we demonstrate that Elo scores are highly sensitive to these parameters. Our findings reveal that varying submission orders can shift scores by 394 points, while contest selection can cause differences of up to 1,122 points for the same model. Run to run performance exhibits substantial instability, with a maximum difference of 349 points in mean scores observed when evaluating identical contests. We conclude that direct Elo comparisons are unreliable and potentially misleading without strict standardization and transparent reporting of experimental settings.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Participants identified key barriers to workflow adoption, including tensions between system generality and domain-specific utility, concerns over long-term sustainability of workflow systems and services, insufficient recognition for those who develop and maintain reproducible workflows, and gaps in standardization, funding, training, and cross-disciplinary collaboration. To address these challenges, the summit proposed action lines spanning technology, policy, and community dimensions: shifting evaluation metrics from raw computational performance toward measuring genuine scientific impact; formalizing workflow patterns and community-driven benchmarks to improve transparency, reproducibility, and usability; cultivating a cohesive international workflows community that engages funding bodies and research stakeholders; and investing in human capital through dedicated workflow engineering roles, career pathways, and integration of workflow concepts into educational curricula and long-term training initiatives. This document presents the summit's findings, beginning with an overview of the current computing ecosystem and the rationale for workflow-centric approaches, followed by a discussion of identified challenges and recommended action lines for advancing scientific discovery through workflows.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了ORACL（Optimized Reasoning for Autoscaling via Chain of Thought with LMLs for Microservices），一种利用先前知识和链式思考来诊断性能回归并推荐资源分配的框架。ORACL将运行时遥测数据转换为语义自然语言状态描述，并调用大型语言模型生成可解释的中间推理路径。这一过程有助于识别潜在的根本原因、精简行动空间，并在政策限制下做出安全的分配决策。

Result: 在代表性的开源微服务工作负载上进行的实验显示，ORACL提高了15%的根因识别准确性，加快了最高达24倍的训练速度，并在短期场景中提升了6%的服务质量，而无需针对特定部署重新训练。

Conclusion: ORACL框架证明了大型语言模型能够在不同微服务部署之间灵活适应，同时提供更准确的故障诊断和更有效的资源分配建议，从而改善了整体服务质量。

Abstract: Applications are moving away from monolithic designs to microservice and serverless architectures, where fleets of lightweight and independently deployable components run on public clouds. Autoscaling serves as the primary control mechanism for balancing resource utilization and quality of service, yet existing policies are either opaque learned models that require substantial per-deployment training or brittle hand-tuned rules that fail to generalize. We investigate whether large language models can act as universal few-shot resource allocators that adapt across rapidly evolving microservice deployments.
  We propose ORACL, Optimized Reasoning for Autoscaling via Chain of Thought with LLMs for Microservices, a framework that leverages prior knowledge and chain-of-thought reasoning to diagnose performance regressions and recommend resource allocations. ORACL transforms runtime telemetry, including pods, replicas, CPU and memory usage, latency, service-level objectives, and fault signals, into semantic natural-language state descriptions and invokes an LLM to produce an interpretable intermediate reasoning trace. This reasoning identifies likely root causes, prunes the action space, and issues safe allocation decisions under policy constraints. Experiments on representative open-source microservice workloads show that ORACL improves root-cause identification accuracy by 15 percent, accelerates training by up to 24x, and improves quality of service by 6 percent in short-term scenarios, without deployment-specific retraining.

### [28] [Proteus: Append-Only Ledgers for (Mostly) Trusted Execution Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05346)
*Shubham Mishra,João Gonçalves,Chawinphat Tankuranand,Neil Giridharan,Natacha Crooks,Heidi Howard,Chris Jensen*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的分布式共识协议Proteus，该协议谨慎地信任TEE的保证，并在CFT协议中嵌入了BFT协议而无需额外的消息传递。Proteus能够在TEE平台受损的情况下仍能保证完整性的同时，保持与常规启用TEE的共识协议相一致的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着行业越来越依赖于分布式账本以提供可信赖的责任归属、强大的完整性保护以及对关键数据的高度可用性，而不集中信任。最近的趋势是采用分层方法，将容错共识与基于硬件的信任执行环境(TEEs)结合来提高韧性。然而，硬件TEE可能遭受（罕见）攻击，从而破坏分布式账本精心设计所要达到的保障。

Method: 为了解决这个问题，研究人员提出了Proteus，这是一种新的分布式共识协议，它通过小心地重构CFT和BFT协议使得两者结构对齐的方式，在不增加额外消息的前提下，谨慎地将一个拜占庭容错(BFT)协议嵌入到容错(CFT)协议之中。

Result: 结果表明，Proteus不仅能够实现在面对TEE平台被攻破时依旧确保数据完整性，同时还能保持与那些常规利用TEE技术的共识协议相当的性能水平。

Conclusion: 综上所述，Proteus代表了一种创新的方法，旨在即使是在TEE安全性受到挑战的情况下也能增强分布式账本系统的可靠性和安全性。

Abstract: Distributed ledgers are increasingly relied upon by industry to provide trustworthy accountability, strong integrity protection, and high availability for critical data without centralizing trust. Recently, distributed append-only logs are opting for a layered approach, combining crash-fault-tolerant (CFT) consensus with hardware-based Trusted Execution Environments (TEEs) for greater resiliency. Unfortunately, hardware TEEs can be subject to (rare) attacks, undermining the very guarantees that distributed ledgers are carefully designed to achieve. In response, we present Proteus, a new distributed consensus protocol that cautiously trusts the guarantees of TEEs. Proteus carefully embeds a Byzantine fault-tolerant (BFT) protocol inside of a CFT protocol with no additional messages. This is made possible through careful refactoring of both the CFT and BFT protocols such that their structure aligns. Proteus achieves performance in line with regular TEE-enabled consensus protocols, while guaranteeing integrity in the face of TEE platform compromises.

### [29] [Reaching Univalency with Subquadratic Communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05356)
*Andrew Lewis-Pye*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本研究通过引入ε-拜占庭协议（ε-BA）来证明达到单一性并不需要二次通信复杂度，而是O(n log n)的通信复杂度。这表明Dolev-Reischuk下界中的二次成本完全来自于结果的传播过程，而不是达成共识的过程。此外，还定义了可提取拜占庭协议，并展示了其可以用O(f log f)的通信复杂度解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨Dolev-Reischuk下界中消息数量的二次成本究竟是为了实现节点间的一致性还是仅仅为了在事后传播结果。

Method: 研究者提出了ε-拜占庭协议的概念，允许一小部分正确的处理器输出错误的结果，并证明当f < n(1/3 - ε)时，该问题可以以O(n log n)的通信复杂度被确定性地解决。此外，他们还定义了一个适用于认证环境下的可提取拜占庭协议模型。

Result: 研究表明，实现一致性本身并不需要二次的消息复杂度；相反，它显示了Dolev-Reischuk下界中的二次成本完全是由后续向所有处理单元传播最终结果所需造成的。对于可提取拜占庭协议，在有认证的情况下，能够以O(f log f)的通信复杂度解决问题。

Conclusion: 结论指出，达到一致性状态的实际通信需求低于先前认为的水平，而大部分的通信开销实际上来源于确保所有正确处理器都得知这个一致性的结果。

Abstract: The Dolev-Reischuk lower bound establishes that any deterministic Byzantine Agreement (BA) protocol for $n$ processors tolerating $f$ faults requires $Ω(f^2+n)$ messages. But what exactly does this quadratic cost pay for? Even the minimal requirement that every correct processor \emph{receive at least one message} already necessitates $Ω(f^2 + n)$ messages. This raises a fundamental question: is the Dolev-Reischuk bound about the difficulty of \emph{reaching univalency} -- the point at which the protocol's outcome is determined -- or merely about \emph{disseminating} the outcome to all processors afterward?
  We resolve this question by showing that reaching univalency does \emph{not} require quadratic communication. Specifically, we introduce $ε$-BA, a relaxation allowing an $ε$-fraction of correct processors to output incorrectly, and prove it can be solved deterministically with $O(n \log n)$ communication complexity when $f < n(1/3 - ε)$. Crucially, any $ε$-BA protocol can serve as the first phase of a full BA protocol: after $ε$-BA, a single all-to-all exchange and majority vote completes BA. Since the outcome is already determined after $ε$-BA, this demonstrates that the quadratic cost in Dolev-Reischuk stems entirely from dissemination, rather than from reaching univalency. We also define Extractable BA for authenticated settings, capturing when processors collectively hold enough signed messages to determine the agreed value, and show it can be solved with communication complexity $O(f \log f)$.

</details>


### [30] [TimelyFreeze: Adaptive Parameter Freezing Mechanism for Pipeline Parallelism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05754)
*Seonghye Cho,Jaemin Han,Hyunjin Kim,Euisoo Jung,Jae-Gil Lee*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为TimelyFreeze的方法，通过将管道调度建模为有向无环图并求解线性程序来计算最优冻结比率，在保证准确性的前提下最小化批次执行时间。实验表明，该方法在LLaMA-8B上实现了高达40%的训练吞吐量提升，并且保持了相当的准确性，适用于多种管道并行设置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的参数冻结技术虽然可以提高训练吞吐量，但往往过度冻结参数，导致不必要的精度下降。

Method: 提出TimelyFreeze方法，它将管道调度过程建模为一个有向无环图(DAG)，并通过求解线性规划问题来找到最佳的冻结比率，以满足精度约束下的最短批处理执行时间。

Result: 实验结果表明，TimelyFreeze可以在不牺牲收敛性和泛化能力的情况下加快大规模模型训练速度，对于LLaMA-8B模型，其训练吞吐量提高了最多40%，同时保持了可比的准确性。

Conclusion: TimelyFreeze提供了一种有效提高基于管道并行的大规模模型训练效率的方法，能够在不影响最终模型性能的前提下显著减少训练所需时间。

Abstract: Pipeline parallelism enables training models that exceed single-device memory, but practical throughput remains limited by pipeline bubbles. Although parameter freezing can improve training throughput by adaptively skipping backward computation, existing methods often over-freeze parameters, resulting in unnecessary accuracy degradation. To address this issue, we propose TimelyFreeze, which models the pipeline schedule as a directed acyclic graph and solves a linear program to compute optimal freeze ratios that minimize batch execution time under accuracy constraints. Experiments show that TimelyFreeze achieves up to 40% training throughput improvement on LLaMA-8B with comparable accuracy. Overall, it enables faster large-scale model training without compromising convergence and generalizes across diverse pipeline-parallel settings.

</details>


### [31] [Location-Aware Dispersion on Anonymous Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05948)
*Himani,Supantha Pandit,Gokarna Sharma*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: This paper introduces LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION, a generalization of the DISPERSION problem where mobile robots must relocate to distinct, similarly colored nodes on a graph. The authors present deterministic algorithms with performance guarantees and provide theoretical limits on the solvability of the problem.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to introduce and solve the LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION problem, which is a more complex version of the well-known DISPERSION problem in distributed robotics. This new problem adds the requirement that robots must settle at nodes of the same color, thus incorporating location awareness into the coordination challenge.

Method: The researchers developed several deterministic algorithms with guaranteed bounds on both time and memory requirements, specifically tailored for the LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION problem. They also provided theoretical analysis including an impossibility result and a lower bound for solving the problem using any deterministic approach.

Result: The research produced deterministic algorithms capable of solving the LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION problem within specific time and memory constraints. Additionally, it set forth an impossibility result and a lower bound, indicating the inherent difficulty of the problem.

Conclusion: The study establishes the algorithmic feasibility of LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION in anonymous networks and highlights the increased challenges in achieving an efficient solution compared to the standard DISPERSION problem. It also provides impossibility results and lower bounds for any deterministic algorithm tackling this new problem.

Abstract: The well-studied DISPERSION problem is a fundamental coordination problem in distributed robotics, where a set of mobile robots must relocate so that each occupies a distinct node of a network. DISPERSION assumes that a robot can settle at any node as long as no other robot settles on that node. In this work, we introduce LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION, a novel generalization of DISPERSION that incorporates location awareness: Let $G = (V, E)$ be an anonymous, connected, undirected graph with $n = |V|$ nodes, each labeled with a color $\sf{col}(v) \in C = \{c_1, \dots, c_t\}, t\leq n$. A set $R = \{r_1, \dots, r_k\}$ of $k \leq n$ mobile robots is given, where each robot $r_i$ has an associated color $\mathsf{col}(r_i) \in C$. Initially placed arbitrarily on the graph, the goal is to relocate the robots so that each occupies a distinct node of the same color. When $|C|=1$, LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION reduces to DISPERSION. There is a solution to DISPERSION in graphs with any $k\leq n$ without knowing $k,n$.
  Like DISPERSION, the goal is to solve LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION minimizing both time and memory requirement at each agent. We develop several deterministic algorithms with guaranteed bounds on both time and memory requirement. We also give an impossibility and a lower bound for any deterministic algorithm for LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION. To the best of our knowledge, the presented results collectively establish the algorithmic feasibility of LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION in anonymous networks and also highlight the challenges on getting an efficient solution compared to the solutions for DISPERSION.

</details>

### [32] [Denoising diffusion networks for normative modeling in neuroimaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.04886)
*Luke Whitbread,Lyle J. Palmer,Mark Jenkinson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出使用去噪扩散概率模型（DDPMs）作为表格式成像衍生表型（IDPs）的统一条件密度估计器，通过采样得出单变量百分位数和偏差分数。研究中使用了两种去噪器主干：一种是基于特征线性调制（FiLM）条件下的多层感知机（MLP），另一种是带有特征自注意力和样本间注意力机制的表格转换器（SAINT）。实验结果表明，在低维度下，扩散模型能够提供与传统基线相当且校准良好的每IDP输出；在高维度下，转换器架构比MLP保持更好的校准度并更好地保留了高阶依赖关系，从而支持可扩展的联合规范模型的发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的神经影像学管道通常为每个成像衍生表型（IDP）单独拟合一个模型，这种方法虽然易于扩展但忽略了可能编码协调模式的多元依赖性。为了克服这一限制，作者提出采用去噪扩散概率模型（DDPMs）来共同估计多个IDP的条件分布，旨在同时捕捉这些生物测量值之间的内在联系，并生成准确可靠的临床解释性偏差得分。

Method: 本研究采用了两种不同的去噪器架构：第一种是结合了特征线性调制（FiLM）技术的多层感知机（MLP），第二种则是集成了特征自注意力机制及跨样本注意力机制的新型表格转换器（SAINT）。这两种方法都通过学习到的嵌入来处理协变量信息。此外，研究还设计了一套全面的评估体系，包括百分位校准、分布保真度测试、多元依赖性诊断以及最近邻记忆分析等，以确保模型性能的有效验证。

Result: 实验结果显示，在较低维度上，提出的扩散模型能够产生与现有基准方法相媲美的单个IDP输出结果，并且能很好地模拟实际存在的依赖结构。当处理更高维度的数据时，基于转换器的方法相较于MLP展现了显著更优的百分位校准能力，并且更有效地保留了数据中的高阶依赖关系。这表明所提方法不仅能够实现精确的个体化偏差评分，同时也为构建大规模联合规范模型提供了可能性。

Conclusion: 通过利用去噪扩散概率模型（DDPMs），特别是采用表格转换器作为核心架构，可以有效地估计复杂多维IDP数据集上的条件密度函数，从而生成经过良好校准的多变量偏差轮廓。这项工作展示了扩散模型在神经影像学领域内开发实用而强大的联合规范建模工具方面的潜力。

Abstract: Normative modeling estimates reference distributions of biological measures conditional on covariates, enabling centiles and clinically interpretable deviation scores to be derived. Most neuroimaging pipelines fit one model per imaging-derived phenotype (IDP), which scales well but discards multivariate dependence that may encode coordinated patterns. We propose denoising diffusion probabilistic models (DDPMs) as a unified conditional density estimator for tabular IDPs, from which univariate centiles and deviation scores are derived by sampling. We utilise two denoiser backbones: (i) a feature-wise linear modulation (FiLM) conditioned multilayer perceptron (MLP) and (ii) a tabular transformer with feature self-attention and intersample attention (SAINT), conditioning covariates through learned embeddings. We evaluate on a synthetic benchmark with heteroscedastic and multimodal age effects and on UK Biobank FreeSurfer phenotypes, scaling from dimension of 2 to 200. Our evaluation suite includes centile calibration (absolute centile error, empirical coverage, and the probability integral transform), distributional fidelity (Kolmogorov-Smirnov tests), multivariate dependence diagnostics, and nearest-neighbour memorisation analysis. For low dimensions, diffusion models deliver well-calibrated per-IDP outputs comparable to traditional baselines while jointly modeling realistic dependence structure. At higher dimensions, the transformer backbone remains substantially better calibrated than the MLP and better preserves higher-order dependence, enabling scalable joint normative models that remain compatible with standard per-IDP pipelines. These results support diffusion-based normative modeling as a practical route to calibrated multivariate deviation profiles in neuroimaging.

</details>

*Yiwen Wang,Jiahao Qin*

Method: DCER框架采用双阶段压缩与基于能量的重构策略。压缩阶段分为模态内频率变换（音频使用小波变换、视频使用DCT）以去除噪音并保留任务相关模式，以及跨模态瓶颈令牌促进真实整合而非特定模态捷径。对于缺失模态的情况，通过学习的能量函数上的梯度下降来恢复表示。

Result: 实验结果表明，在CMU-MOSI、CMU-MOSEI及CH-SIMS数据集上，DCER框架达到了最先进的性能水平，并显示出一种U形鲁棒性模式，在完全信息和高缺失率情况下对多模态融合特别有利。此外，最终能量值还能提供内在不确定性量化（与预测误差的相关性超过0.72）。

Conclusion: 提出的DCER框架有效地解决了多模态融合中存在的噪声输入和模态缺失两大挑战，通过创新性的双阶段压缩和基于能量的重建技术，在多个基准测试中均取得了领先表现。

Abstract: Multimodal fusion faces two robustness challenges: noisy inputs degrade representation quality, and missing modalities cause prediction failures. We propose DCER, a
  unified framework addressing both challenges through dual-stage compression and energy-based reconstruction. The compression stage operates at two levels:
  within-modality frequency transforms (wavelet for audio, DCT for video) remove noise while preserving task-relevant patterns, and cross-modality bottleneck tokens
  force genuine integration rather than modality-specific shortcuts. For missing modalities, energy-based reconstruction recovers representations via gradient descent
  on a learned energy function, with the final energy providing intrinsic uncertainty quantification (\r{ho} > 0.72 correlation with prediction error). Experiments on
  CMU-MOSI, CMU-MOSEI, and CH-SIMS demonstrate state-of-the-art performance across all benchmarks, with a U-shaped robustness pattern favoring multimodal fusion at
  both complete and high-missing conditions. The code will be available on Github.

This duality is our cornerstone contribution -- by injecting kinematic momentum, we sidestep the topological depth constraint ($L \geq 2$) for induction head formation. While standard architectures require two layers for induction from static positions, our extension grants direct access to velocity, enabling Single-Layer Induction and Spectral Forensics via Bode Plots. ### [38] [Physics as the Inductive Bias for Causal Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.04907)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 通过结合物理知识与数据驱动方法，所提出的框架能够在动态系统中更准确地恢复因果关系，同时提高了估计结果的稳定性和物理一致性。

Abstract: Causal discovery is often a data-driven paradigm to analyze complex real-world systems. In parallel, physics-based models such as ordinary differential equations (ODEs) provide mechanistic structure for many dynamical processes. Integrating these paradigms potentially allows physical knowledge to act as an inductive bias, improving identifiability, stability, and robustness of causal discovery in dynamical systems. However, such integration remains challenging: real dynamical systems often exhibit feedback, cyclic interactions, and non-stationary data trend, while many widely used causal discovery methods are formulated under acyclicity or equilibrium-based assumptions. In this work, we propose an integrative causal discovery framework for dynamical systems that leverages partial physical knowledge as an inductive bias. Specifically, we model system evolution as a stochastic differential equation (SDE), where the drift term encodes known ODE dynamics and the diffusion term corresponds to unknown causal couplings beyond the prescribed physics. We develop a scalable sparsity-inducing MLE algorithm that exploits causal graph structure for efficient parameter estimation. Under mild conditions, we establish guarantees to recover the causal graph. Experiments on dynamical systems with diverse causal structures show that our approach improves causal graph recovery and produces more stable, physically consistent estimates than purely data-driven state-of-the-art baselines.

### [39] [Temporal Pair Consistency for Variance-Reduced Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.04908)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的连续时间生成模型通常采用独立处理每个时间点的目标函数进行训练，这导致了高估计方差和低效的采样问题。

Method: 引入了一种轻量级的方差减少原则——时间配对一致性（TPC），它通过在相同的概率路径上连接不同时间点的速度预测来工作，完全作用于估计器层面而无需更改模型架构、概率路径或求解器。

Abstract: Continuous-time generative models, such as diffusion models, flow matching, and rectified flow, learn time-dependent vector fields but are typically trained with objectives that treat timesteps independently, leading to high estimator variance and inefficient sampling. Prior approaches mitigate this via explicit smoothness penalties, trajectory regularization, or modified probability paths and solvers. We introduce Temporal Pair Consistency (TPC), a lightweight variance-reduction principle that couples velocity predictions at paired timesteps along the same probability path, operating entirely at the estimator level without modifying the model architecture, probability path, or solver. We provide a theoretical analysis showing that TPC induces a quadratic, trajectory-coupled regularization that provably reduces gradient variance while preserving the underlying flow-matching objective. Instantiated within flow matching, TPC improves sample quality and efficiency across CIFAR-10 and ImageNet at multiple resolutions, achieving lower FID at identical or lower computational cost than prior methods, and extends seamlessly to modern SOTA-style pipelines with noise-augmented training, score-based denoising, and rectified flow.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的直接偏好优化（DPO）等方法在处理语言模型根据成对偏好进行对齐时存在固定参考策略导致分布不匹配及错误偏好信号放大等问题；而无参考变体虽然避免了不匹配但可能遇到不受限制的奖励漂移。

Method: 开发了Geometric Anchor Preference Optimization (GAPO) 方法，使用相对于当前策略的小范围内的对抗性局部扰动作为动态、几何感知的锚点，实现基于局部敏感性的自适应重加权机制。此外定义了“锚点差距”，即策略与其锚点之间的奖励差异，并证明在平滑条件下它近似于最坏情况下的局部边际退化。

Result: GAPO 在多种噪声环境下持续提高了鲁棒性，同时在标准LLM对齐和推理基准上达到了与现有方法相当或更好的性能。

Conclusion: GAPO 提供了一种有效解决偏好对齐中分布不匹配和奖励漂移问题的新途径，通过利用动态几何感知锚点和基于锚点差距的优化目标，实现了更鲁棒的语言模型偏好学习。

Abstract: Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) and related methods align large language models from pairwise preferences by regularizing updates against a fixed reference policy. As the policy drifts, a static reference, however, can become increasingly miscalibrated, leading to distributional mismatch and amplifying spurious preference signals under noisy supervision. Conversely, reference-free variants avoid mismatch but often suffer from unconstrained reward drift. We propose Geometric Anchor Preference Optimization (GAPO), which replaces the fixed reference with a dynamic, geometry-aware anchor: an adversarial local perturbation of the current policy within a small radius that serves as a pessimistic baseline. This anchor enables an adaptive reweighting mechanism, modulating the importance of each preference pair based on its local sensitivity. We further introduce the Anchor Gap, the reward discrepancy between the policy and its anchor, and show under smoothness conditions that it approximates worst-case local margin degradation. Optimizing a logistic objective weighted by this gap downweights geometrically brittle instances while emphasizing robust preference signals. Across diverse noise settings, GAPO consistently improves robustness while matching or improving performance on standard LLM alignment and reasoning benchmarks.

</details>

*Arno Geimer,Beltran Fiz Pontiveros,Radu State*

Method: 提出了FedRandom方法，该方法将贡献度评估中的不稳定性看作是统计估计问题，通过增加样本数量来改善估计质量。具体来说，FedRandom允许产生比传统联邦学习策略更多的样本点，以此来获得更稳定且精确的贡献度量。

Result: 研究者们通过对包括CIFAR-10、MNIST在内的多个数据集进行测试后发现，FedRandom方法能够显著降低贡献度评估结果与真实值之间的差距——在一半以上的评估场景中减少了超过三分之一的距离；同时，在超过90%的情况下增强了评估结果的稳定性。

Conclusion: FedRandom为联邦学习环境中存在的贡献度评估不稳定性问题提供了一个有效的解决方案，不仅提高了贡献度衡量的准确性，也增强了系统整体的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Federated Learning is a privacy-preserving decentralized approach for Machine Learning tasks. In industry deployments characterized by a limited number of entities possessing abundant data, the significance of a participant's role in shaping the global model becomes pivotal given that participation in a federation incurs costs, and participants may expect compensation for their involvement. Additionally, the contributions of participants serve as a crucial means to identify and address potential malicious actors and free-riders. However, fairly assessing individual contributions remains a significant hurdle. Recent works have demonstrated a considerable inherent instability in contribution estimations across aggregation strategies. While employing a different strategy may offer convergence benefits, this instability can have potentially harming effects on the willingness of participants in engaging in the federation. In this work, we introduce FedRandom, a novel mitigation technique to the contribution instability problem. Tackling the instability as a statistical estimation problem, FedRandom allows us to generate more samples than when using regular FL strategies. We show that these additional samples provide a more consistent and reliable evaluation of participant contributions. We demonstrate our approach using different data distributions across CIFAR-10, MNIST, CIFAR-100 and FMNIST and show that FedRandom reduces the overall distance to the ground truth by more than a third in half of all evaluated scenarios, and improves stability in more than 90% of cases.
